 chunaav ayog ne kiye ye 11 ahm badlaav1
 ) For the first time, electronic voting machines ie evms will be accounted for on paper trail for the votes cast in the entire state
 yah vyavastha us sawaal kaa jawaab he ki iviem kaa batan dabaae jane par aawaaj to aati he, par vot dala yaa nahin iskaa pataa nahin chalata
 The voter will now have the facility of voter verifiable paper audit trail ie VVPAT
 isamen vot daalane ke baad atm kii tarah iviem se bhi kaagaj kii parchi niklegi
 This slip will be visible to the voter for about 15 seconds and then fall in the compartment inside the machine
 upi kii 403 siton ke liye saat charnon main chunaav, jaane kab kahaan?2
 ) The Election Commission will send to each voter's house a polling slip containing the photo of voters
 is baar vah parchi sirf parchi nahin, balki votaron kaa pahchaan patr bhi rahegaa

e

 ) For the first time in the assembly elections of these five states, there will be a 30 inch high voting compartment made of plastic sheets like steel gray flakes around the voting machine
 ise us teble par chaaron ore lagaaya jayega, jahaan iviem rahegi

 aise main matadaata ke sir or ankhon se ye pataa chal jaataa tha ki vot kise diya gaya he

 7

 aise chaar poster har matdaan centre par lagenge

e

 america adhikariyon ne yah jaankaree di
 Acting Revenue Deputy Minister of Terrorism and Financial Intelligence Adam Zubin said, "during the reign of Kim Jong Un, North Korea has tortured millions of its people, including extrajudicial killings, forced labor and torture
" ' mantralay ne kaha ki uttar korea ke sheersh netaa kim desh ke grih suraksha tathaa lok suraksha maamalon ke pramukh kii apni bhoomika main maanavadhikaron ke hanan ke liye jimmedaar hai
 According to officials in Washington, 'north Korea's Ministry of Home Security placed 80,000 to 120,000 prisoners in political prisoner camps, sentenced them to death, sexually harassed, starved, and made them work as slaves
 is
 ' america ne kaha he ki kim kii nigaraanee main kaam karne vaala lok suraksha mantralay police steshnon, hiraasat kendron or shram shiviron kaa ek aisa network chalaata he, jahaan sandigdhon ko poochtacha ke liye rakhaa jaataa he or unhen pratadit kiya jaataa he

 US officials say the report clearly states that Kim is ultimately responsible for most human rights violations

 ) Putting Kim on the black list for the first time, the US said that it was to take cognizance that North Korea was "one of the world's most oppressive countries
" ' pratibandhon kii suchi main kim tathaa das anya sheersh adhikariyon ke naamon ko shaamil kiya gaya he or aarope he ki ye log desh main raajnneetik kaidi shiviron main raajnneetik kaidiyon ko pratadit karne or hatyaon samet gambhir maanavadhikaron ke hanan main shaamil rahe hai

 The ministry said that North Korea's top leader Kim is responsible for human rights abuses in his role as the country's head of home security and public security affairs
